beginSubroutine: s32'OnActionBegin'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFWalk'

    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)

  endIf:

  endIf:

  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  if: Mem(IsTrainingMode)
    getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_TST', 2, 157
    if: Mem(TrainingValue)
      if: Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA)
        isObjectActive: (STACK3)
        ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
          if: Mem(BattleDoing)
            createObject: s32'Marking', (ENEMY_CENTER)
            stackObject: (STACK3), (PREVIOUS)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK0)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    exPointFReset: (PLAYER), -160000, 500000
    createObject: s32'CrowNeutral', (EX_POINT_F)
    stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X_FRONT), (SELF), (CENTER), (STACK0), (CENTER)
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(-180000)
    calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X_FRONT), (SELF), (CENTER), (STACK0), (CENTER)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(-140000)
      calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_Y), (SELF), (CENTER), (STACK0), (CENTER)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(280000)
        calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_Y), (SELF), (CENTER), (STACK0), (CENTER)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(320000)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(IsLand)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
    ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_TST', 2, 157
            ifNot: Mem(TrainingValue)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(-1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'GraveRiperFunc'
  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_AtkLv3', Val(2), Val(2), Val(0), Val(0)
  callSubroutine: s32'cmn_countertype_middle_slash'
  pushbackX: 150
  pushbackXForHit: 60
  hitAirPushbackX: Val(15000)
  hitAirPushbackY: Val(30000)
  hitEffectSlash: 1
  groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(15000)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(35000)
    counterhitAirPushbackX: Val(35000)
    counterhitAirPushbackY: Val(20000)
    upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK_GROUNDED)
      hitAirPushbackX: Val(15000)
      hitAirPushbackY: Val(25000)
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    pushbackX: 70
    atkAngle: 70
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(10000)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(40000)
    upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK_GROUNDED)
      hitAirPushbackX: Val(15000)
      hitAirPushbackY: Val(30000)
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(20000)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(20000)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(4)
    pushbackX: 50
    atkAngle: -70
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(15000)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(25000)
    rollDuration: 10
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'GraveRiperHoldCheck'
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg4), Val(0)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_S)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_H)
    endElse: 
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (IDLING)
    if: Mem(ActReg0)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      if: Mem(ActReg3)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(18)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(25)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
        endIf: 
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'atk'
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'GraveRiperDamage'
  damage: Val(43)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    damage: Val(48)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
    damage: Val(53)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'MarkingAtkCheck'
  upon: (PARRY)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (ATTACK_COLLISION_MAIN_PLAYER)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PARRY)
  endUpon: 
  upon: (ATTACK_COLLISION_MAIN_PLAYER)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (ATTACK_COLLISION_MAIN_PLAYER)
    sendSignalToAction: s32'Marking', (SIGNAL0)
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'ArbiterSign_AtkPosCheck'
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(500000)
    exPointFReset: (FLOOR_CENTER), 500000, 0
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(1000000)
      exPointFReset: (FLOOR_CENTER), 1000000, 0
    endIf: 
    else: 
      exPointFReset: (ENEMY_LAND), 0, 0
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg0)
    exPointFReset: (EX_POINT_F), 0, 0
  endIf: 
  else: 
    exPointFReset: (EX_POINT_F), 0, 0
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'WildAssault'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_WildAssault', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    wallBlowoffType: (BLOWOFF_SLIDE)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-450000)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg2), Val(0)
    callSubroutine: s32'MarkingAtkCheck'
    displayMesh: s32'Cape', 1
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'tst360_00', 3
  sprite: s32'tst360_01', 3
  voiceLine: s16'vxxx350'
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'tst360_02', 3
  sprite: s32'tst360_03', 3
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
  beginLabel: s32'attack'
  sprite: s32'tst360_04', 3
  sprite: s32'tst360_05', 3
  sprite: s32'tst360_06', 3
  haltMomentum: 1

endState:
